constexpr int kTensorArenaSize = 16 * 1024;
static uint8_t tensor_arena[kTensorArenaSize];

int main() {
  printf("Hello from %s!\n", MYNAMESTR);

  const tflite::Model* model = tflite::GetModel(g_hello_world_float_model_data);
  if (model->version() != TFLITE_SCHEMA_VERSION) {
    fprintf(stderr, "Model schema %d != supported %d\n", model->version(), TFLITE_SCHEMA_VERSION);
    return 1;
  }

  tflite::AllOpsResolver resolver;
  tflite::MicroInterpreter interpreter(model, resolver, tensor_arena, kTensorArenaSize);
  if (interpreter.AllocateTensors() != kTfLiteOk) {
    fprintf(stderr, "AllocateTensors() failed\n");
    return 1;

cat > src/hello_world_float_model_data.h << 'EOF'
#ifndef HELLO_WORLD_FLOAT_MODEL_DATA_H
#define HELLO_WORLD_FLOAT_MODEL_DATA_H
extern const unsigned char g_hello_world_float_model_data[];
extern const int g_hello_world_float_model_data_len;
#endif
EOF

# 2) Make sure the source includes the header
grep -n 'hello_world_float_model_data.h' src/hello_world_float_model_data.cc || \
  sed -i '1i #include "hello_world_float_model_data.h"' src/hello_world_float_model_data.cc

# 3) Rename symbols to what hello_world.cc expects, and make them const/int
sed -i 's/\bunsigned char\b \+hello_world_float_tflite\[\]/const unsigned char g_hello_world_float_model_data[]/' src/hello_world_float_model_data.cc
sed -i 's/\bunsigned int\b \+hello_world_float_tflite_len/const int g_hello_world_float_model_data_len/' src/hello_world_float_model_data.cc

# 4) Rebuild
make clean
make -j1

// Register 3 ops: FC + Quantize + Dequantize
tflite::MicroMutableOpResolver<3> resolver;
resolver.AddFullyConnected();
resolver.AddQuantize();
resolver.AddDequantize();

// after AllocateTensors():
TfLiteTensor* input  = interpreter.input(0);
TfLiteTensor* output = interpreter.output(0);

// helpers for quantization
auto to_int8 = [](float f, float s, int zp)->int8_t {
  int32_t q = (int32_t)std::round(f / s) + zp;
  if (q < -128) q = -128; if (q > 127) q = 127;
  return (int8_t)q;
};
auto to_float = [](int8_t q, float s, int zp)->float {
  return (int(q) - zp) * s;
};

// when setting input each step:
if (input->type == kTfLiteFloat32) {
  input->data.f[0] = x;
} else if (input->type == kTfLiteInt8) {
  input->data.int8[0] = to_int8(x, input->params.scale, input->params.zero_point);
} else { fprintf(stderr,"Unsupported input type %d\n", input->type); return 1; }

} else { fprintf(stderr,"Unsupported output type %d\n", output->type); return 1; }nt);

usage: git config [<options>]

Config file location
    --[no-]global         use global config file
    --[no-]system         use system config file
    --[no-]local          use repository config file
    --[no-]worktree       use per-worktree config file
    -f, --[no-]file <file>
                          use given config file
    --[no-]blob <blob-id> read config from given blob object

Action
    --[no-]get            get value: name [value-pattern]
    --[no-]get-all        get all values: key [value-pattern]
    --[no-]get-regexp     get values for regexp: name-regex [value-pattern]
    --[no-]get-urlmatch   get value specific for the URL: section[.var] URL
    --[no-]replace-all    replace all matching variables: name value [value-pattern]
    --[no-]add            add a new variable: name value
    --[no-]unset          remove a variable: name [value-pattern]
    --[no-]unset-all      remove all matches: name [value-pattern]
    --[no-]rename-section rename section: old-name new-name
    --[no-]remove-section remove a section: name
    -l, --[no-]list       list all
    --[no-]fixed-value    use string equality when comparing values to 'value-pattern'
    -e, --[no-]edit       open an editor
    --[no-]get-color      find the color configured: slot [default]
    --[no-]get-colorbool  find the color setting: slot [stdout-is-tty]

Type
    -t, --[no-]type <type>
                          value is given this type
    --bool                value is "true" or "false"
    --int                 value is decimal number
    --bool-or-int         value is --bool or --int
    --bool-or-str         value is --bool or string
    --path                value is a path (file or directory name)
    --expiry-date         value is an expiry date

Other
    -z, --[no-]null       terminate values with NUL byte
    --[no-]name-only      show variable names only
    --[no-]includes       respect include directives on lookup
    --[no-]show-origin    show origin of config (file, standard input, blob, command line)
    --[no-]show-scope     show scope of config (worktree, local, global, system, command)
    --[no-]default <value>
                          with --get, use default value when missing entry
